\subsection{Core}\label{subsec:blocks_core}
These blocks are the most essential blocks in the game.
            The game relies on these blocks to exist and on their IDs to be fixed.
\newline
\subsubsection{Air}\label{subsubsec:blocks_core_air}
The air block that fills the world. Could also be interpreted as "no block".
\newline
\begin{tabular}{ll}
Named ID
 & \texttt{Air}
\\
ID
 & \texttt{0}
\\
State Count
 & 1
\\
Opaque
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
Mesh At Non Opaques
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
Solid
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
Unshaded
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
Collider
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
Trigger
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
Interactable
 &  \XSolidBrush \\
\end{tabular}
\newline
Behaviors:
\newline
\begin{tabular}{ll}
Unmeshed
 & —
\\
Static
 & —
\\
Fillable
 & —
\\
\end{tabular}

\subsection{Environment}\label{subsec:blocks_environment}
These blocks make up most of the environment and thus are essential for world generation.
\newline
\subsubsection{Grass}\label{subsubsec:blocks_environment_grass}
Soil with some grass on top. Plants can be placed on top of this.
                The grass can burn, creating ash.
\newline
\begin{tabular}{ll}
Named ID
 & \texttt{Grass}
\\
ID
 & \texttt{4}
\\

 & 1

\subsection{Stones}\label{subsec:blocks_stones}
All sorts of stone types. Stone occurs naturally in the world but can also be used for the construction of various things.
\newline
\subsubsection{Granite}\label{subsubsec:blocks_stones_granite}
Granite is found next to volcanic activity.
                When carved, the patterns show geometric shapes.

\subsubsection{Pumice}\label{subsubsec:blocks_stones_pumice}
Pumice is created when lava rapidly cools down, while being in contact with a lot of water.
                When carved, the patterns depict heat rising from the earth.

\subsection{Metals}\label{subsec:blocks_metals}
All sorts of metals and their ores, as well as other metal-related blocks.
\newline
\subsubsection{Iron}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_iron}
Iron is the metal with the elemental symbol Fe.
\newline
\subsubsection{Gold}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_gold}
Gold is the metal with the elemental symbol Au.
\newline
\subsubsection{Silver}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_silver}
Silver is the metal with the elemental symbol Ag.
\newline
\subsubsection{Platinum}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_platinum}
Platinum is the metal with the elemental symbol Pt.
\newline
\subsubsection{Copper}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_copper}
Copper is the metal with the elemental symbol Cu.
\newline
\subsubsection{Aluminum}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_aluminum}
Aluminum is the metal with the elemental symbol Al.
\newline
\subsubsection{Lead}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_lead}
Lead is the metal with the elemental symbol Pb.
\newline
\subsubsection{Tin}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_tin}
Tin is the metal with the elemental symbol Sn.
\newline
\subsubsection{Mercury}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_mercury}
Mercury is the metal with the elemental symbol Hg.
\newline
\subsubsection{Zinc}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_zinc}
Zinc is the metal with the elemental symbol Zn.
\newline
\subsubsection{Chromium}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_chromium}
Chromium is the metal with the elemental symbol Cr.
\newline
\subsubsection{Manganese}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_manganese}
Manganese is the metal with the elemental symbol Mn.
\newline
\subsubsection{Titanium}\label{subsubsec:blocks_metals_titanium}
Titanium is the metal with the elemental symbol Ti.
\newline

Nickel is the metal with the elemental symbol Ni.
